                         1500sqft Carriage House located at the Hidden Vineyard Estate. With fully equipped Kitchen, Family Room &amp; TV, Master Bedroom with Cal King bed &amp; TV , 2nd breezeway bedroom/office with a Twin Day bed and additional luxury twin folding bed available.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="550">
                         Located on 2nd story of the detached 4 car garage at the Hidden Vineyard Estate this 1500sqft 2 bedroom 1 bath apartment is a prefect complement if you are looking to house 24 people on one property since the Main Estate at Hidden Vineyard can sleep up to 20. Or if you are looking for an estate that has 6 private bedrooms, as the main home has 5 bedrooms and the Guest House has a 1 private bedroom or even a additional 7th bedroom if you count the breezeway bedroom. Carriage House at Hidden Vineyard is also a prefect get away for a week or even a month if it is just for 1 or 2 people. This luxury apartment is full furnished with 2 TV's, Kitchen with Granite Counter tops, oven, stove, microwave, dishwasher and more! The Family Room is equipped with a sofa. The breeze bedroom or office has a day twin bed and a built in desk, the master bedroom does have a Cal King Bed. There is 1 bathroom with tub/shower combo and the views of all of the windows of this carriage house are amazing! All you see is vineyards all the way around you! If renting the carriage house with the main home then guests will have access to the main home pool &amp; spa. If renting the Carriage Home alone there is no access to the main home pool/spa. We do have several areas to sit out and enjoy the views all around and the Carriage House does have it's own BBQ Grill. This Carriage House is amazing and prefect fit when staying in Temecula Wine Country.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="551">
                         Hidden Vineyard Estate is located in Temecula Wine Country and surrounded by not only the properties own vineyard but neighboring Wineries Vineyards as well. Our home is walking distance from such Wineries as Carter Estate, South Coast, Ponte, Wiens, Lorimar. We are just 5 minutes or less from all the Temecula Wineries and just 10 minutes from Old Town Temecula. All car services are available for pick up at our estate.

                        <div data-reactid="1112">
                         A cute attached guest house with its own entrance. kitchenette, bathroom. Great location close to restaurants, old town, wineries and Temecula Mall.

                         Great quiet family neighborhood.

                        <div data-reactid="1115">
                         <li data-reactid="1116"><p data-reactid="1117">The listing is advertised as is and is pretty accurate. Great location. However, when booking, host seems to be picky with whom he lets stay at his place (understandably so) but if you're more of the type who prefers to just book a place, pay, little interaction with host, then you're better off doing an instant book. For how much we spoke with the host, the communication wasn't the greatest. Host seemed to have forgotten how many guests were staying and made us feel a bit uncomfortable when we arrived after making a few remarks in regards to it, although we have the texts and airbnb messages as proof stating the number of guests that would be in our party, and had already paid. Also wanted us out an hour to 30 minutes prior to the check out time listed. We abided out of respect but it would have been nice otherwise. We didn't ended staying over night because we opted to stay at a friend's closer to the wineries. We were there during the day though and all seemed well otherwise. I think this would have been a good stay had in not been for the miscommunication.</p><span data-reactid="1118">steffanie</span><span data-reactid="1119">2017-03-26T00:00:00Z</span></li>

                        <div data-reactid="1200">
                         I have a great house in beautiful Temecula calif. know for their many wineries located about 40 miles north of San Diego and one hour southwest of palm springs and two hours from Los Angeles. I can now rent 2 bedrooms and sometimes 3 for those who have extra family and friends. The house has 2 1/2 bathrooms. Guests will have full run and use of the house; except for my bedroom. My backyard oversees a beautiful golf course in the upscale redhawk community. Guests also have access to the back yard with hottub an and upstairs patio balcony. Great place for cocktails in the evening. There is also a gas grill for your use if u need one. i have internet cable and can provide you suggestions for entertainment, dining etc. I have a great place for anyone traveling and wanting a safe, affordable ultra clean private residence facing the 11th green of the Redhawk golf course. if you like to walk i am about 1 mile from shopping an restaurants. Also about a mile from Pechanga casino and about 5 miles away from the wineries and about 10 minutes to the historic old town with its many fine restaurants and clubs. Lastly I am pet friendly and will welcome fido with open paws for a small fee. ($10 per nite) I pride myself in making your stay a memorable and totally relaxing experience. You can book the rooms under the heading "King Bedroom/office" The other room can be found under the heading "Queen bedroom/mini retreat". I look forward to hosting you in the near future.
